        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          margin: auto;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





repro:



<span class="line"><!---->repro:<!----></span>



<br>





** you need to add any note to poc1.html before run poc.html



<span class="line"><!---->** you need to add any note to poc1.html before run poc.html<!----></span>



<br>





1. download asan-linux-release-1040850.zip and unzip



<span class="line"><!---->1. download asan-linux-release-1040850.zip and unzip<!----></span>



<br>





2. start a http server in the folder of poc.html and poc1.html



<span class="line"><!---->2. start a http server in the folder of poc.html and poc1.html<!----></span>



<br>





3. run `./chrome --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel --user-data-dir=/your/profile/path/ --disable-popup-blocking 



<span class="line"><!---->3. run `./chrome --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel --user-data-dir=/your/profile/path/ --disable-popup-blocking <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html`



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html`"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html`<!----></a>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





4. browser crash



<span class="line"><!---->4. browser crash<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





`FrameUserNoteChanges` has a raw_ptr `rfh` but don't observe its lifetime[1]. Unfortunately, we can free this `rfh` before using it.



<span class="line"><!---->`FrameUserNoteChanges` has a raw_ptr `rfh` but don't observe its lifetime[1]. Unfortunately, we can free this `rfh` before using it.<!----></span>



<br>





`rfh` is passed from `CalculateNoteChanges`[2], it is generated by `document.AsRenderFrameHostIfValid()` (1). Although document is a weak ptr, the `rfh` is still a raw_ptr. So its lifetime is not guaranteed.



<span class="line"><!---->`rfh` is passed from `CalculateNoteChanges`[2], it is generated by `document.AsRenderFrameHostIfValid()` (1). Although document is a weak ptr, the `rfh` is still a raw_ptr. So its lifetime is not guaranteed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

> "you need to add any note to poc1.html before run poc.html"



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; "you need to add any note to poc1.html before run poc.html"<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





you can add a note to poc1.html like this:



<span class="line"><!---->you can add a note to poc1.html like this:<!----></span>



<br>





1 $> ./chrome --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel --user-data-dir=/your/profile/path/ --disable-popup-blocking 



<span class="line"><!---->1 $&gt; ./chrome --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel --user-data-dir=/your/profile/path/ --disable-popup-blocking <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc1.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc1.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc1.html<!----></a>



<br>





2 right click and choose 'add note'



<span class="line"><!---->2 right click and choose 'add note'<!----></span>



<br>





3 save the note in side panel



<span class="line"><!---->3 save the note in side panel<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





> Does triggering the bug require the use of the nonstandard flags --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel?



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; Does triggering the bug require the use of the nonstandard flags --enable-features=UserNotes,UnifiedSidePanel?<!----></span>



<br>





yes, these flags are needed.



<span class="line"><!---->yes, these flags are needed.<!----></span>

[user-notes] Fix UAF when attaching a note



<span class="line"><!---->[user-notes] Fix UAF when attaching a note<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Frame note changes are computed after note metadata is fetched. The



<span class="line"><!---->Frame note changes are computed after note metadata is fetched. The<!----></span>



<br>





changes includes a reference to the frame they're applied to. However,



<span class="line"><!---->changes includes a reference to the frame they're applied to. However,<!----></span>



<br>





there's another async step when the note models are fetched (and indeed,



<span class="line"><!---->there's another async step when the note models are fetched (and indeed,<!----></span>



<br>





yet another async step when the changes are applied and the notes are



<span class="line"><!---->yet another async step when the changes are applied and the notes are<!----></span>



<br>





being attached).



<span class="line"><!---->being attached).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





We need to user a weak reference to the render frame host (the document



<span class="line"><!---->We need to user a weak reference to the render frame host (the document<!----></span>



<br>





actually, since we should abort even if the RFH lives on but was



<span class="line"><!---->actually, since we should abort even if the RFH lives on but was<!----></span>



<br>





navigated to a different document). This CL changes FrameUserNoteChanges



<span class="line"><!---->navigated to a different document). This CL changes FrameUserNoteChanges<!----></span>



<br>





to store a WeakDocumentPtr.



<span class="line"><!---->to store a WeakDocumentPtr.<!----></span>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Hi and thanks for your note and question. While the mitigation is minimal and the UI interaction required is reasonable in the expected workflow/ use of this feature, this issue is not remote exploitable and is reliant on user interaction to achieve triggering this bug. The classification of which falls at the higher reward end of the mildly/lightly mitigated security bug category in our reward rubric, thus the $7,000 reward.



<span class="line"><!---->Hi and thanks for your note and question. While the mitigation is minimal and the UI interaction required is reasonable in the expected workflow/ use of this feature, this issue is not remote exploitable and is reliant on user interaction to achieve triggering this bug. The classification of which falls at the higher reward end of the mildly/lightly mitigated security bug category in our reward rubric, thus the $7,000 reward.<!----></span>
